*  Israeli Minister of Defense Israel Katz has declared that the military will remain in these camps throughout the coming year, and that the residents will not be allowed to return. [[02:16:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8218.3s)]
*  Mr. President, esteemed members of the Court, UNGA adopted Resolution 79-232 on December 19, 2024, requesting the ICJ to render an advisory opinion based on Article 96 of the UN Charter and Article 65 of the Statute of the Court. [[02:17:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8231.3s)]
*  This resolution sought an advisory opinion from the ICJ to clarify Israel's obligations as an occupying power and as a UN member in relation to the presence and activities of the UN, [[02:17:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8254.3s)]
*  including its agencies and bodies, other international organizations, and third states in relation to OPT. [[02:17:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8270.3s)]
*  Turkey has submitted a written statement pursuant of the Court's order of February 27, 2025, in accordance with Article 66, paragraph 2 of the Statute of the ICJ. [[02:17:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8279.3s)]
*  Turkey's support for this request underscores its commitment to ensuring that Israel adheres to its international obligations. [[02:18:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8294.3s)]
*  Among these, obligations is the responsibility to allow unimpeded access to humanitarian aid, essential supplies, and basic services for the Palestinian civilian population in the OPT. [[02:18:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8304.3s)]
*  Additionally, Israel is required to facilitate the work of international organizations. [[02:18:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8320.3s)]
*  As a UN member, Israel must act in good faith to fulfill its obligations under the Security Council and UNGA resolutions, [[02:18:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8326.3s)]
*  which include compliance with the UN Charter and the requirement to implement UN Security Council resolutions. [[02:18:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8336.3s)]
*  Turkey's position is anchored in key international legal instruments, including the UN Charter, international humanitarian law, and international human rights law. [[02:19:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8345.3s)]
*  Several principles are particularly relevant in evaluating Israel's obligations in the OPT. [[02:19:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8358.3s)]
*  Under Articles 2, paragraph 3 and 2, 4 of the UN Charter, all member states, including Israel, are obliged to resolve disputes peacefully and refrain from the threat or use of force. [[02:19:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8366.3s)]
*  These obligations extend to cooperating with the UN in maintaining global peace and security, ensuring that international norms are upheld. [[02:19:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8383.3s)]
*  The privileges and immunities granted to the UN, its agencies, and personnel are essential for ensuring their independent and impartial functioning. [[02:19:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8395.3s)]
*  They stem from the 1946 Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the UN. [[02:20:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8407.3s)]
*  Turkey underlines their importance, particularly in the context of humanitarian operations in the OPT. [[02:20:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8413.3s)]
*  The inviolability of UN organizations is crucial for their ability to assist the Palestinian refugees effectively. [[02:20:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8421.3s)]
*  Israel, as the occupying power in the OPT, is bound by the Fourth Geneva Convention of 1949, which stipulates the protection and welfare of civilians under occupation. [[02:20:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8431.3s)]
*  These obligations include ensuring that humanitarian aid reaches the Palestinian population without obstruction, respecting the presence and work of the UN, international organizations, and third states providing aid and upholding the rights of Palestinians under international humanitarian and human rights law. [[02:20:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8444.3s)]
*  Turkey maintains that Israel's compliance with these obligations is necessary for achieving peace and stability in the region. [[02:21:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8467.3s)]
*  The basis for responding to the questions brought before the court for an advisory opinion is the State of Israel's UN membership, which is yet to be accorded to the State of Palestine as per foundational UN resolutions. [[02:21:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8478.3s)]
*  During the 207th plenary meeting of the UN in 1948, Moshe Sharet, the Israeli Foreign Minister of the time, reaffirmed Israel's commitment to the UN principles emphasizing peace, cooperation with neighboring Arab states, and adherence to international obligations. [[02:21:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8495.3s)]
*  Israel assured that its policies align with the UN Charter and relevant resolutions, leading to its recognition as a peace-loving state willing and able to uphold its obligations. [[02:21:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8516.3s)]
*  However, despite its commitments, Israel has not implemented UNGA resolutions, obstructed the establishment of a Palestinian state as outlined in UNGA Resolution 181, and denied refugees their rights under Resolution 194. [[02:22:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8530.3s)]
*  These violations continue to challenge Israel's adherence to its UN obligations, particularly as more countries recognize Palestine as a state. [[02:22:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8549.3s)]
*  Article 4, one of the UN Charter, sets five conditions for membership. Being a state, being peace-loving, accepting the Charter's obligations, having the ability to carry them out, and demonstrating willingness to do so. [[02:22:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8561.3s)]
*  The ICJ affirmed these criteria is an advisory opinion, underscoring that UN membership requires continuous compliance with the Charter's principles. [[02:22:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8579.3s)]
*  Failure to uphold these obligations may lead to accountability under international law. [[02:23:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8591.3s)]
*  UNGA and UN Security Council resolutions stress the need for states to protect UN personnel and facilities, particularly in conflict zones. [[02:23:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8598.3s)]
*  UNGA Resolution 57-337 reaffirmed the safety of UN personnel, while UN Security Council Resolution 1502 condemned attacks against them as violations of international law. [[02:23:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8609.3s)]
*  Additionally, UN Security Resolution 22-86 specifically condemned attacks on medical personnel and facilities during armed conflicts, urging member states to safeguard humanitarian actors. [[02:23:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8626.3s)]
*  Furthermore, the 1946 Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the UN explicitly guarantees the inviolability of UN premises, archives, and assets, ensuring the organization's ability to operate independently and fulfill its mandate. [[02:24:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8643.3s)]
*  Under the Geneva Conventions, which both Israel and Palestine are parties to, civilians and humanitarian personnel must be protected during conflicts. [[02:24:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8663.3s)]
*  Common Article 3 stipulates humane treatment for those not actively engaged in hostilities, including UN staff. [[02:24:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8675.3s)]
*  The ICJ has ruled that the Geneva Conventions apply to all occupied territories, rejecting Israel's claim that they do not apply the Yure to the OPT. [[02:24:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8684.3s)]
*  Articles 104 and 105 of the UN Charter further reinforce the legal protections afforded to the UN, granting it legal personality and ensuring its ability to function without state interference. [[02:24:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8698.3s)]
*  Israel, as a party to the 1946 Convention, is obliged to respect these provisions. [[02:25:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8716.3s)]
*  Moreover, Article 2.5 of the Charter requires Israel to assist in the UN in its activities rather than to obstruct them. [[02:25:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8723.3s)]
*  Israel, having ratified these provisions without reservations, is legally bound to respect UN premises, personnel, and missions. [[02:25:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8734.3s)]
*  These privileges are granted to ensure that the UN can effectively carry out its mandate. [[02:25:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8745.3s)]
*  Despite these obligations, Israel has restricted access of UN personnel in the OPT, including East Jerusalem. [[02:25:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8753.3s)]
*  The Independent International Commission of Inquiry on the OPT has reported Israeli non-cooperation in UN investigations, blocking entry of officials and medical professionals. [[02:26:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8762.3s)]
*  The Special Rapporteur on the situation of human rights in the OPT noted that Israel's refusal to grant access to UN investigators may constitute obstruction of justice. [[02:26:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8776.3s)]
*  The Office of the High Commissioner for Human Rights has also reported that Israel denies visas to international staff working in the OPT. [[02:26:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8790.3s)]
*  The ICJ has emphasized the importance of UN immunity and the obligation of states to respect and protect UN personnel. [[02:26:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8800.3s)]
*  The 1949 Advisory Opinion on the Reparation for Injuries Suffered in the Service of the UN affirmed that attacks on UN agents hinder the organization's mission and constitute violations of international law. [[02:26:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8811.3s)]
*  The ICJ recognized the UN's right to claim reparations for injuries suffered by its personnel and upheld the principle of implied powers, [[02:27:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8828.3s)]
*  which allows the UN to take necessary actions to fulfill its duties, even if not explicitly stated in the Charter. [[02:27:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=8840.3s)]

*  on its natural resources and wealth, [[03:12:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11560.140000000001s)]

*  with the Palestinian authorities. [[03:12:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11572.140000000001s)]
*  The Knesset has adopted a declaration indicating that it opposes the creation of a Palestinian state, [[03:12:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11576.54s)]
*  and this one day before your court gives its advisory opinion in July 2024. [[03:13:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11583.1s)]
*  This declaration of the Israeli Parliament is once again in flagrant contradiction [[03:13:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11591.1s)]
*  with the rights of the Palestinian people to self-determination. [[03:13:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11596.380000000001s)]
*  All the state bodies of Israel have the obligation to respect these rights [[03:13:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11600.7s)]
*  and not to make obstacles to its implementation. [[03:13:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11606.060000000001s)]
*  In this sense, the obligation exists to avoid any legislative or administrative disposition [[03:13:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11609.34s)]
*  to prevent the implementation of the right to self-determination. [[03:13:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11617.02s)]
*  Mr. President, ladies and gentlemen, [[03:13:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11622.380000000001s)]
*  nothing justifies the maintenance of the Israeli occupation on the Palestinian people [[03:13:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11624.86s)]
*  that prevents them from exercising their right to self-determination. [[03:13:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11630.460000000001s)]
*  The first relevant obligation is therefore to respect these rights and to stop their violation. [[03:13:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11633.74s)]
*  It is through the strict respect of international law, [[03:14:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11641.98s)]
*  and not through expansionism, oppression or force, that we can solve the problem. [[03:14:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11646.3s)]

*  First, Israel's obligation to respect the privileges and immunities of the United Nations. [[03:15:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11727.82s)]
*  Israel recognized in the exchange of letters with UNRWA of 1967 [[03:15:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11736.94s)]
*  that a number of facilities were essential for the agency to operate effectively. [[03:15:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11742.94s)]
*  The fact that Israel recognized these facilities as essential indicates that they are, [[03:15:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11750.62s)]
*  pursuant to Article 105 of the Charter, necessary for the fulfillment of UNRWA's purposes. [[03:15:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11758.140000000001s)]
*  The General Assembly has recalled that the agency, [[03:16:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11768.140000000001s)]
*  as a subsidiary organ of the United Nations, [[03:16:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11772.78s)]
*  enjoys the benefits of the Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the United Nations. [[03:16:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11777.099999999999s)]
*  The main provisions of the General Convention, anyway, reflect customary international law. [[03:16:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11785.82s)]
*  I will deal with three of these. [[03:16:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11793.339999999998s)]
*  The immunity from every form of legal process set forth in Section 2 [[03:16:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11799.259999999998s)]
*  is essential for the independent exercise by UNRWA of its functions. [[03:16:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11805.42s)]
*  The inviolability of UNRWA premises set forth in Section 3 guarantees that the premises [[03:16:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11813.1s)]
*  may not be entered and that the United Nations must itself be permitted to control activities [[03:17:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11821.18s)]
*  occurring on those premises. [[03:17:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11828.86s)]
*  All UNRWA officials enjoy immunity and the privileges set forth in Section 18. [[03:17:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11832.54s)]
*  The provisions relating to officials in the General Convention apply to all staff members, [[03:17:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11840.94s)]
*  the only exception being those recruited locally and assigned to hourly rates. [[03:17:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11848.060000000001s)]
*  In this case, those criteria are cumulative. [[03:17:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11854.7s)]
*  The immunity of UNRWA from every form of legal process and the inviolability of its premises [[03:17:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11862.460000000001s)]
*  are absolute. [[03:17:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11871.58s)]
*  They may not be qualified or overridden by military expediency or national security. [[03:17:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11874.78s)]
*  Israel has an absolute obligation to respect the privileges and immunities of the United Nations. [[03:18:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11885.66s)]
*  Israel self-evidently has an obligation in Teralia not to enter UNRWA premises, [[03:18:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11893.980000000001s)]
*  not to damage or destroy such premises, not to detain UNRWA staff without charge or trial, [[03:18:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11903.18s)]
*  and not to seek to extirpate the agency from the occupied Palestinian territory. [[03:18:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11912.46s)]
*  Second, the text of Article 2, paragraph 5 of the Charter is to the effect that Israel has a [[03:18:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11921.74s)]
*  general obligation to give every assistance to the United Nations. [[03:18:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11931.74s)]
*  State practice, including that of Israel itself, confirms this. [[03:18:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11936.3s)]
*  The contention by Israel that the obligation relates only to enforcement action taken [[03:19:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11944.619999999999s)]
*  by the Security Council has no basis in international law. [[03:19:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11951.34s)]
*  The interpretation for which Israel now contends runs counter to the clear wording of Article 2, [[03:19:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11957.82s)]
*  5 and is inconsistent with the court's interpretation in the reparations case. [[03:19:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11965.099999999999s)]
*  Israel has an obligation to give UNRWA every assistance in any action it takes, [[03:19:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11973.74s)]
*  pursuant to the provisions of the Charter. [[03:19:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11981.259999999998s)]
*  There is a further aspect. [[03:19:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11986.619999999999s)]
*  Judge Lauterpacht was correct in the voting procedure, where he observed that a state which [[03:19:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11987.98s)]
*  ignores a series of General Assembly resolutions acts at its peril when a point is reached, [[03:19:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=11997.34s)]
*  when the cumulative effect of the persistent disregard of the articulate opinion of the [[03:20:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12008.06s)]
*  organization is such as to foster the conviction that the state in question has become guilty of [[03:20:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12014.14s)]
*  disloyalty to the principles and purposes of the Charter. [[03:20:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12021.66s)]
*  Israel is obliged under the Charter to give due consideration in good faith [[03:20:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12033.099999999999s)]
*  to the resolutions of the General Assembly. [[03:20:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12039.1s)]

*  It applies no less to the Charter. [[03:20:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12053.42s)]
*  Israel has the obligation to give due regard to General Assembly resolutions, [[03:20:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12058.78s)]
*  notably those adopted in the 10th Emergency Special Session. [[03:21:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12064.94s)]
*  Third, one of the purposes of the United Nations is, according to Article 1, paragraph 3 of the [[03:21:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12071.9s)]
*  Charter, to achieve international cooperation in solving international problems of a humanitarian [[03:21:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12079.26s)]
*  character. As Judge El-Arian observed, the principle of international cooperation in Article 1, [[03:21:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12087.98s)]
*  paragraph 3, is, like the other purposes and principles of the United Nations, a legal [[03:21:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12097.74s)]
*  principle, binding on states. The Charter recognizes this in Article 14, to which the court was taken [[03:21:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12105.74s)]
*  this morning, and which addresses the situation of a violation of the provisions of the present [[03:21:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12115.5s)]
*  Charter, setting forth the purposes and principles of the United Nations. [[03:22:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12124.86s)]
*  This obligation to cooperate was developed in greater detail in the Friendly Relations [[03:22:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12135.1s)]
*  Declaration. Its fourth principle lays down the duty of states to cooperate with one another [[03:22:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12140.46s)]
*  in accordance with the Charter. [[03:22:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12148.46s)]
*  Israel's obligations as regards the safety and security of United Nations personnel. [[03:22:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12156.46s)]
*  Israel has obligations in this regard under the rules of customary international law, [[03:22:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12163.82s)]
*  codified in the Convention on the Safety of United Nations and Associated Personnel. [[03:22:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12169.34s)]
*  That this Convention codifies customary international law is evident from the fact that [[03:22:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12177.82s)]
*  the General Assembly adopted it by consensus. Notable in this regard is Israel's obligation [[03:23:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12184.779999999999s)]
*  to facilitate the unimpeded transit of UNRWA and other United Nations personnel across its own territory. [[03:23:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12193.18s)]
*  This obligation includes unimpeded transit from one part of the occupied Palestinian territory to another. [[03:23:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12205.18s)]
*  Israel also has the obligation to ensure the safety and security of United Nations personnel, [[03:23:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12215.18s)]
*  to release detained personnel and to penalise crimes against them. [[03:23:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12223.18s)]
*  Israel has, finally, the obligation not to make UNRWA or other United Nations personnel the object of an attack, [[03:23:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12231.18s)]
*  or any other action that prevents them from discharging their mandate. [[03:24:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12241.18s)]
*  That, Mr. President, members of the Court, concludes my presentation. I thank you and ask that you invite Professor Alfredo Crosato to the podium. [[03:24:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12251.18s)]

*  Thank you, Mr. President, members of the Court. It is an honour to appear before you on behalf of Jordan. [[03:24:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12267.18s)]
*  I shall now focus on Israel's obligations concerning humanitarian relief in Gaza. [[03:24:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12273.18s)]
*  These arise from a variety of sources that include the Law of Occupation, Human Rights Law, [[03:24:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12279.18s)]
*  the Law on the Protection of Persons in the Event of Disasters, and these courts' orders on provisional measures. [[03:24:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12283.18s)]
*  All told, international law requires Israel to provide humanitarian relief to the civilian population of Gaza, [[03:24:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12290.18s)]
*  a territory which is at present far from adequately supplied. Indeed, a humanitarian catastrophe is already unfolding. [[03:24:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12297.18s)]
*  Where Israel is unable or unwilling to fulfil its duties, it must facilitate relief schemes undertaken by third parties. [[03:25:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12305.18s)]
*  Time is of the essence, and Israel must do so swiftly and in cooperation with the third parties involved in good faith. [[03:25:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12315.18s)]
*  Let me start with the Law of Occupation and two general remarks. [[03:25:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12322.18s)]
*  First, the Court recently reaffirmed that the Law of Occupation applies to the entire Palestinian territory, including Gaza. [[03:25:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12326.18s)]
*  That situation has not changed, and any contention that Israel does not currently occupy Gaza must be rejected. [[03:25:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12333.18s)]
*  Israel has not been liberated from its obligations as an occupying power. [[03:25:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12341.18s)]
*  Second, the scope of Israel's claimed authority as an occupying power. [[03:25:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12345.18s)]
*  Whatever the situation, international law does not confer such an authority or discretion allowing a state to circumvent obligations aimed at ensuring the survival of a civilian population. [[03:25:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12350.18s)]
*  It is impossible to conceive a good faith interpretation... [[03:26:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12363.18s)]
*  I'm sorry to interrupt you, but could you speak more slowly? [[03:26:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12367.18s)]
*  Sure, thank you very much. [[03:26:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12370.18s)]
*  It is impossible to conceive a good faith interpretation of the Law of Occupation, [[03:26:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12371.18s)]
*  consistent with its object and purpose, that would result in widespread suffering of civilians and destruction of civilian objects. [[03:26:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12376.18s)]
*  The Court has determined that Israel's occupation is illegal. [[03:26:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12384.18s)]
*  Its policies and practices, I quote, [[03:26:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12390.18s)]
*  manifest an intention to create a permanent and irreversible Israeli presence in the OPT, [[03:26:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12392.18s)]
*  breaching the provision of acquisition of territory by force and the principle of self-determination. [[03:26:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12398.18s)]
*  You also found that Israel has engaged in a sustained abuse of its position as an occupying power. [[03:26:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12404.18s)]
*  Any territorial control still exercised by Israel until it has withdrawn must therefore ensure the well-being of Palestinians and respect for the right to self-determination. [[03:26:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12411.18s)]
*  Moreover, since Israel has been abusing the Law of Occupation, it cannot claim broad rights or powers arising from it. [[03:27:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12422.18s)]
*  This is a core legal consequence of the general principle prohibiting the abuse of rights. [[03:27:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12431.18s)]
*  Israel's relevant obligations are primarily found in the Fourth Geneva Convention and customary international law. [[03:27:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12437.18s)]
*  As long as Israel occupies Gaza, the customary rule reflected in Article 43 of the Hague regulations requires it to act for the benefit of the local population. [[03:27:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12443.18s)]
*  This is a general guiding principle and fundamental duty of Israel. [[03:27:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12454.18s)]
*  In addition, Article 55 of the Fourth Geneva Convention requires Israel, to the fullest extent of the means available to it, [[03:27:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12459.18s)]
*  to ensure the food and medical supplies of the population, including by bringing in the necessary foodstuffs, medical stores and other articles, [[03:27:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12467.18s)]
*  if the resources of the occupied territory are inadequate. [[03:27:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12475.18s)]
*  Article 69 of the Additional Protocol 1, which reflects custom, expands the range of supplies that must be provided. [[03:27:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12479.18s)]
*  Under Article 56, Israel must ensure and maintain the medical and hospital establishments and services, public health and hygiene, [[03:28:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12486.18s)]
*  and allow medical personnel of all categories to carry out their duties. [[03:28:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12494.18s)]
*  Article 50 mandates the facilitation of the proper working of all institutions devoted to the care and education of children. [[03:28:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12499.18s)]
*  The Convention also contains key provisions concerning third parties when the Occupy Empower does not or cannot fulfill the obligations I just mentioned. [[03:28:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12508.18s)]
*  Where Israel fails to act, civilians are not left to their own fate without more. [[03:28:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12517.18s)]
*  Article 59 stipulates that if the occupied territory is inadequately supplied, the Occupy Empower shall agree to relieve schemes on behalf of the population [[03:28:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12523.18s)]
*  and shall facilitate them by all the means at its disposal. [[03:28:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12533.18s)]
*  These schemes may be undertaken by states or by impartial humanitarian organizations, [[03:28:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12537.18s)]
*  and shall consist in particular of the provision of consignments, of foodstuffs, medical supplies and clothing. [[03:29:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12543.18s)]
*  These are erroneous obligations of both result and conduct. [[03:29:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12550.18s)]
*  Israel cannot oppose those relief schemes. [[03:29:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12554.18s)]
*  Agreement is the required outcome, no exception. [[03:29:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12557.18s)]
*  Israel must also facilitate those schemes using all available means. [[03:29:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12561.18s)]
*  This is a high standard of conduct consistent with the gravity of the situation that Article 59 addresses, [[03:29:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12567.18s)]
*  prohibiting Israel from actions or omissions that may hinder humanitarian relief. [[03:29:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12574.18s)]
*  Article 59 must be read together with Article 1, [[03:29:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12580.18s)]
*  which contains states undertaking to respect and to ensure respect for the Convention in all circumstances. [[03:29:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12585.18s)]
*  Every state party must ensure compliance by Israel with its obligations, while respecting, of course, other rules of international law. [[03:29:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12591.18s)]
*  Article 59 is a form of application of Article 1, a means for states to ensure compliance with Israel's relief obligations. [[03:29:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12598.18s)]
*  When states seek to provide relief schemes, individually or jointly, [[03:30:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12613.18s)]
*  they do not do so only by virtue of an option envisaged by Article 59. [[03:30:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12617.18s)]
*  They have an obligation to act of their own. [[03:30:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12622.18s)]
*  Article 59 may require practical arrangements for the orderly supply of humanitarian relief. [[03:30:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12625.18s)]
*  Insofar as these are needed, Israel must consider them in good faith, bearing in mind the needs of civilians. [[03:30:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12632.18s)]
*  If the arbitrary or unjustified delays would not be consistent with Article 59, they would defeat the purpose of the obligation. [[03:30:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12639.18s)]
*  In the present circumstances, Jordan, like virtually all participants, considers that Gaza is inadequately supplied, [[03:30:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12646.18s)]
*  this is manifest, and that Israel's obligations have been triggered. [[03:30:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12653.18s)]
*  Jordan is also of the firm view that UNRWA meets the principles of impartiality and neutrality, [[03:30:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12659.18s)]
*  as confirmed recently by the Colona report and the OIOS investigations. [[03:31:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12665.18s)]
*  Furthermore, there is no other actor that could realistically replace the agency and its mandates to provide and distribute humanitarian relief and other services in Gaza. [[03:31:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12670.18s)]
*  Israel must therefore allow UNRWA to continue its humanitarian operations and cease all conduct which prevents the agency from doing so. [[03:31:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12683.18s)]
*  There is no other way to give full effect to Article 59 of the Convention in the circumstances. [[03:31:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12691.18s)]
*  Israel's obligations, as we noted, also arise from other sources. [[03:31:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12698.18s)]
*  These are separate obligations which complement and are as stringent as the law of occupation. [[03:31:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12702.18s)]
*  I will address a few key ones. [[03:31:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12708.18s)]
*  Israel must ensure the right to life of Palestinians consistent with the ICCPR and the Convention on the Rights of the Child, which apply in Gaza. [[03:31:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12711.18s)]
*  This includes a positive duty to take action to prevent foreseeable harm or injury that may result in arbitrary deprivation of life. [[03:32:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12720.18s)]
*  In the present context, such risk is not only foreseeable but already materialized. [[03:32:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12729.18s)]
*  To avoid further loss of life, Israel must strictly respect the fundamental principles of IHL and facilitate humanitarian relief in Gaza. [[03:32:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12735.18s)]
*  The Covenant on Economic, Social and Cultural Rights requires Israel to ensure the right to an adequate standard of living, [[03:32:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12745.18s)]
*  the right to the highest attainable standard of physical and mental health, and the right to education. [[03:32:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12752.18s)]
*  These rights are at risk of being altogether denied to Palestinians in Gaza, [[03:32:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12759.18s)]
*  and Israel must take immediate action and allow the supply of relief to prevent such denial. [[03:32:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12764.18s)]
*  Jordan has also referred to the law on the protection of persons in the event of disasters, recently codified by the ILC. [[03:32:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12772.18s)]
*  The obligations in this area are closely linked to those under human rights law, [[03:33:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12780.18s)]
*  and require Israel, among others, to cooperate in good faith with third parties, to facilitate humanitarian assistance, and not to arbitrarily withhold consent to such assistance. [[03:33:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12785.18s)]
*  Finally, Israel has obligations arising from the interim measures in the South Africa-Israel case. [[03:33:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12797.18s)]
*  It must take all necessary and effective measures to enable the unhindered provision of basic services and humanitarian assistance in Gaza. [[03:33:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12803.18s)]
*  It must do so as a matter of urgency, without delay, and in cooperation with the United Nations. [[03:33:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12812.18s)]
*  The obligations we have addressed should be interpreted and applied in a systemic manner, [[03:33:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12820.18s)]
*  and against the background of the principle of self-determination, which is of paramount importance. [[03:33:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12825.18s)]
*  Time, again, is of the essence, and Israel must perform its duties swiftly and in good faith. [[03:33:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12832.18s)]
*  The horror that Palestinian civilians are undergoing in Gaza must stop. [[03:33:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12839.18s)]
*  Mr. President, members of the Court, this concludes my presentation and Jordan's oral submissions. [[03:34:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12845.18s)]
*  We thank you for your kind attention in these important proceedings. [[03:34:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12849.18s)]
*  I thank the representatives of Jordan for their presentation. [[03:34:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=12853.18s)]

*  as the fundamental mechanism through which the legitimate rights [[03:37:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13075.18s)]

*  Excuse me again, Your Honour, but please speak more slowly. [[03:38:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13112.18s)]
*  Sorry? [[03:38:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13116.18s)]
*  Please speak more slowly. [[03:38:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13117.18s)]
*  Slowly. [[03:38:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13119.18s)]
*  That address emphasized the imperative necessity of holding the occupying power accountable [[03:38:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13120.18s)]
*  through the mechanisms of international law, including international humanitarian law, [[03:38:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13127.18s)]

*  In February 2024, Kuwait, along with several states, stood before this Honourable Court, [[03:39:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13141.18s)]
*  condemning the occupying powers prolonged in legal occupation of Palestinian lands. [[03:39:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13148.18s)]
