*  unequivocally affirmed that the occupying powers' occupation is unlawful and must end as rapidly as possible. [[03:39:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13161.18s)]
*  Yet, the relentless continuation of military operations, [[03:39:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13171.18s)]
*  including devastating aerial strikes on Gaza since 18 March 2025, [[03:39:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13175.18s)]
*  stands as a distressing testament to this ongoing injustice. [[03:39:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13181.18s)]
*  In parallel, the occupying powers' actions have severely imperiled the vital humanitarian mission of UNRWA. [[03:39:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13187.18s)]
*  Recent legislative actions enacted by the occupying power in January 2025 [[03:39:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13196.18s)]
*  have severely curtailed UNRWA's capacity to function, [[03:40:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13202.18s)]
*  critically undermining its ability to deliver indispensable support and services to Palestinian civilians. [[03:40:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13206.18s)]
*  Kuwait's oral submission is structured thematically to facilitate the Court's careful consideration of the applicable legal frameworks. [[03:40:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13215.18s)]
*  I will begin by confirming the Court's jurisdiction and clarifying the scope of the question and relevant law. [[03:40:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13224.18s)]
*  I will then highlight the occupying powers' violations of the privileges and immunities of the UN and UNRWA. [[03:40:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13232.18s)]
*  Finally, I will address the breaches of international humanitarian and human rights law. [[03:40:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13240.18s)]
*  This structured approach is intended to provide the Court with a clear and coherent legal foundation [[03:40:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13246.18s)]
*  for its advisory opinion. [[03:40:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13253.18s)]
*  Mr. President, Members of the Court, [[03:40:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13255.18s)]
*  this inquiry is urgent and essential. [[03:40:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13258.18s)]
*  The Court's authoritative guidance is vital to relieving immediate suffering and reaffirming international law. [[03:41:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13262.18s)]
*  Mr. President, Honourable Members of the Court, [[03:41:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13270.18s)]
*  with your permission, I shall now address briefly, but with the requisite care, [[03:41:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13273.18s)]
*  the question of whether the Court possesses jurisdiction in the present advisory proceedings [[03:41:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13279.18s)]
*  and whether it should exercise that jurisdiction. [[03:41:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13285.18s)]
*  The legal basis is beyond doubt. [[03:41:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13289.18s)]
*  The Court's jurisprudence is clear, and the urgency of the matter before you could not be greater. [[03:41:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13292.18s)]
*  The advisory jurisdiction of this Court is grounded in two foundational provisions. [[03:41:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13299.18s)]
*  Article 96, one of the UN Charter, and Article 65, one of the Statutes of the Court. [[03:41:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13305.18s)]
*  Article 96 authorizes the UN General Assembly to request an advisory opinion from this Court on any legal question. [[03:41:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13313.18s)]
*  Article 65, in turn, enables the Court to respond to such requests, [[03:42:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13322.18s)]
*  provided they are made by an organ duly authorized under the UN Charter. [[03:42:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13328.18s)]
*  These two provisions form the legal cornerstone of the Court's advisory function. [[03:42:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13334.18s)]
*  They leave no room for doubt. [[03:42:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13340.18s)]
*  The request presently before the Court originates from the General Assembly. [[03:42:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13344.18s)]
*  Moreover, the question it poses is unmistakably legal. [[03:42:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13349.18s)]
*  Specifically, it asks whether that conduct of the occupying power complies with the rules and principles of international law, [[03:42:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13354.18s)]
*  including international humanitarian law, international human rights law, [[03:42:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13362.18s)]
*  and the 1946 Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the UN. [[03:42:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13367.18s)]
*  It directly concerns the UN, its agencies, and other international actors, [[03:42:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13372.18s)]
*  as it relates to their operations and the protection of their personnel in and in relation to the OPT. [[03:42:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13378.18s)]
*  The great minority of participants in these proceedings have suggested that the political context surrounding this request [[03:43:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13387.18s)]
*  undermines its legal character and the clarity of the question. [[03:43:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13395.18s)]
*  But this Court has long and consistently held otherwise. [[03:43:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13400.18s)]
*  As reaffirmed in the Court's jurisprudence, the presence of political aspects in a question does not deprive it of its character as a legal question. [[03:43:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13405.18s)]
*  Indeed, this Court was created precisely to answer legal questions that arise even and especially within politically sensitive contexts. [[03:43:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13415.18s)]
*  It is true that Article 65 of the Statutes uses permissive languages. [[03:43:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13427.18s)]
*  The Court may render an advisory opinion. [[03:43:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13432.18s)]
*  That implies discretion. [[03:43:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13435.18s)]
*  But the Court's own jurisprudence makes clear that this discretion is not absolute. [[03:43:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13438.18s)]
*  The Court has emphasized that responding to such requests forms part of its participation in the work of the UN, [[03:44:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13444.18s)]
*  and that it should not, in principle, refuse to respond unless compelling or, in the Court's own language, decisive reasons are present. [[03:44:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13452.18s)]
*  In this context, it is essential to recall that the General Assembly's request does not invoke Section 30 of the 1946 Convention, [[03:44:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13464.18s)]
*  which governs the settlement of disputes between the UN and Member States. [[03:44:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13474.18s)]
*  As explained in Kuwait's written statement, the request does not concern such a dispute. [[03:44:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13479.18s)]
*  Rather, it seeks clarification of the occupying power's legal obligations, particularly as they relate to the presence and activities of the UN [[03:44:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13485.18s)]
*  and other international actors in and in relation to the OPT. [[03:44:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13495.18s)]
*  Finally, it shall be made clear that rendering an advisory opinion could in no way compromise the Court's judicial integrity in pending cases against the occupying power before this Court. [[03:45:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13501.18s)]
*  Kuwait categorically rejects this view. [[03:45:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13515.18s)]
*  The Court's advisory and contentious functions are clearly distinct. [[03:45:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13519.18s)]
*  Independence of a related case cannot deprive the General Assembly of its right to request an advisory opinion. [[03:45:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13524.18s)]
*  Also, in the present advisory proceedings, the divergence of legal views specifically concerns the actions of the UN and its organs [[03:45:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13532.18s)]
*  in relation to the occupying power's obligations as UN member and as the occupying power in the OPT. [[03:45:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13542.18s)]
*  Mr. President, Members of the Court, the question is legal, and it falls squarely within the ambit of Articles 65 and 96. [[03:45:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13551.18s)]
*  Nothing prevents the Court from rendering an advisory opinion to the contrary. [[03:46:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13562.18s)]
*  The gravity of the situation makes the Court's guidance not only appropriate, but indispensable. [[03:46:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13567.18s)]
*  Excuse me, the interpreter is having a problem, so please speak slowly. [[03:46:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13574.18s)]
*  Mr. President, I will now address the scope of the questions submitted by the General Assembly and the relevant legal framework governing the Court's analysis. [[03:46:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13583.18s)]
*  The present request is distinct from last year's advisory opinion, focusing on specific legal questions. [[03:46:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13594.18s)]
*  The General Assembly does not seek a comprehensive account of all obligations of the occupying power as a UN member, [[03:46:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13602.18s)]
*  but rather an opinion on its duties concerning the presence and activities of the UN, its organs, agencies such as ANUWA, [[03:46:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13611.18s)]
*  other international organizations, and third states and in relation to the OPT. [[03:47:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13621.18s)]
*  This includes measures such as legislation aimed at banning ANUWA. [[03:47:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13628.18s)]
*  General Assembly Resolution 79-232 recalls the occupying power's obligation to ensure unrestricted humanitarian assistance, [[03:47:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13635.18s)]
*  essential services, and support for the Palestinian people's right to self-determination. [[03:47:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13647.18s)]
*  Paragraph 10 of the resolution establishes a coherent legal framework referencing relevant sources, [[03:47:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13654.18s)]
*  the UN Charter, international humanitarian and human rights law, the law governing privileges and immunities of international organizations, [[03:47:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13662.18s)]
*  pertinent resolutions of the Security Council, the General Assembly, the Human Rights Council, [[03:47:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13672.18s)]
*  and this Court's advisory opinions from 2004 and 2024. [[03:47:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13679.18s)]
*  In Kuwait's view, this list is explicitly non-exhaustive. [[03:48:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13686.18s)]
*  As underlined by at least 25 participants in these proceedings, [[03:48:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13692.18s)]
*  it includes the Convention on the Rights of the Child to which the occupying power is a party, [[03:48:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13697.18s)]
*  given the disproportionate and devastating impact of the conflict on Palestinian children, [[03:48:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13704.18s)]
*  as well as the Court's binding provision measures in the genocide case wrote by South Africa against the occupying power, [[03:48:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13710.18s)]
*  a valid point highlighted by a great number of participants. [[03:48:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13719.18s)]
*  Mr. President, Members of the Court, [[03:48:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13726.18s)]
*  I shall now turn to the legal obligations incumbent upon the occupying power concerning the privileges and immunities of the UN, [[03:48:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13730.18s)]
*  with particular attention to Anwar. [[03:49:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13740.18s)]
*  The privileges and immunities enjoyed by the UN are firmly grounded in Article 105 of the UN Charter. [[03:49:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13743.18s)]
*  These privileges and immunities constitute essential protections, [[03:49:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13752.18s)]
*  enabling the UN to perform its mandate independently and effectively, free from interference. [[03:49:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13757.18s)]
*  Importantly, these protections apply not only to the UN as an entity, [[03:49:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13765.18s)]
*  but extend comprehensively to its representatives, officials, personnel, and assets. [[03:49:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13772.18s)]
*  Consequently, the occupying power bears a clear and unequivocal legal obligation to uphold and respect these privileges and immunities. [[03:49:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13780.18s)]
*  This obligation is explicitly reinforced and codified by the 1946 Convention, [[03:49:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13790.18s)]
*  which remains fully applicable and binding upon the occupying power due to its ongoing membership in the UN. [[03:49:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13798.18s)]
*  The 1946 Convention establishes a comprehensive legal framework to safeguard the functioning of the organization. [[03:50:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13807.18s)]
*  It guarantees inter-alien, the immunity of UN property from interference, the inviolability of its premises, [[03:50:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13815.18s)]
*  the freedom of movement of officials and expert on mission, and legal immunity for acts performed in unofficial capacity. [[03:50:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13825.18s)]
*  These protections extend equally to the UN specialized agencies and programs, including UNRWA. [[03:50:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13834.18s)]
*  Significantly, in the 1967 exchange of letters between UNRWA and the occupying power, [[03:50:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13842.18s)]
*  the latter expressly undertook to fully cooperate with UNRWA's humanitarian activities in both the West Bank and the Gaza Strip. [[03:50:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13850.18s)]
*  These privileges and immunities impose a binding obligation on the occupying power to allow UNRWA to function fully in its territory and in the OPT. [[03:51:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13861.18s)]
*  They cannot be unilaterally revoked. [[03:51:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13872.18s)]
*  Furthermore, Article 103 of the UN Charter ensures that obligations under the Charter prevail over any conflicting international norms. [[03:51:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13875.18s)]
*  Accordingly, and as Quaid and 20 other participants have underscored, [[03:51:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13887.18s)]
*  justification based on military necessity or national security cannot override the privileges and immunities accorded to the UN. [[03:51:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13893.18s)]
*  Despite these obligations, the occupying power has passed legislation that came into force in January 2025, [[03:51:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13905.18s)]
*  explicitly prohibiting UNRWA's operations and banning official contact with its representatives. [[03:51:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13914.18s)]
*  This law severely hinders UNRWA's capacity to operate in the OPT. [[03:52:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13921.18s)]
*  Not only by prohibiting engagement, but by obstructing the issuance of permits required for personnel movement and aid delivery. [[03:52:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13927.18s)]
*  Such measures constitute a clear violation of the occupying power's obligations under international law. [[03:52:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13937.18s)]
*  The inviolability of UN premises, the cornerstone of both Article 105 of the UN Charter and Section 3 of the 1946 Convention, [[03:52:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13947.18s)]
*  prohibits any forced entry, interference or attack on UN facilities. [[03:52:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13957.18s)]
*  This protection extends beyond physical inviolability to include immunity from domestic legal jurisdiction. [[03:52:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13964.18s)]
*  Yet, the occupying power has repeatedly violated this principle by targeting UN humanitarian facilities with military strikes and clear breach of its obligations. [[03:52:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13973.18s)]
*  In addition, the freedom of movement of UN officials is enshrined in Article 1 of the 1946 Convention. [[03:53:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13987.18s)]
*  These provisions prohibit immigration restrictions or administrative barriers that would obstruct UN operations. [[03:53:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=13996.18s)]
*  Nevertheless, the occupying power has denied entry to UN officials, barred the UN Secretary General, and declared senior UN personnel persona non grata. [[03:53:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14004.18s)]
*  These actions not only obstruct the UN's functions, but also violate both treaty-based and customary international law. [[03:53:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14017.18s)]
*  Mr. President, UN officials and experts on mission also enjoy functional immunity for acts performed in the course of their official duties. [[03:53:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14026.18s)]
*  This immunity includes protection from legal proceedings and procedural safeguards, such as the right to visitation and fair treatment in case of detention. [[03:53:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14037.18s)]
*  However, the occupying power has detained UN personnel for statements made and acts performed in their official capacities, violating Section 18 of the 1946 Convention. [[03:54:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14049.18s)]
*  In particular, the arbitrary detention of UNO staff has denied the UN the ability to communicate with or visit its personnel, thereby undermining their independence. [[03:54:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14064.18s)]
*  Quaid submits that the occupying power has consistently violated its international legal obligations relating to the privileges and immunities of the UN. [[03:54:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14078.18s)]
*  Such conduct is not merely unlawful. It endangers the effective functioning of the UN within and in relation to the OPT. [[03:54:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14091.18s)]
*  Quaid therefore respectfully calls upon the Court to reaffirm the inviolability of the UN and its agencies and to clarify the legal consequences arising from the occupying power's persistent noncompliance. [[03:55:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14101.18s)]
*  Mr. President, Members of the Court, I will now turn to the obligations of the occupying power under international humanitarian law and international human rights law as they apply to the OPT. [[03:55:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14119.18s)]
*  The Court has consistently reaffirmed that international humanitarian law applies to the OPT. [[03:55:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14133.18s)]
*  In its 2024 advisory opinions, the Court confirmed the applicability of the Geneva Convention relative to the protection of civilian persons in time of war and the 1907 Hague regulations as binding legal frameworks. [[03:55:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14141.18s)]
*  The occupying power, by virtue of its continued military presence and effective control over the territory, remains fully bound by these provisions. [[03:55:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14159.18s)]
*  First, under Article 50 of the Fourth Geneva Convention, the occupying power must ensure the proper functioning of educational institutions, particularly those serving children. [[03:56:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14170.18s)]
*  The systematic targeting of UNRWA schools and the displacement of students has gravely disrupted education in the OPT. [[03:56:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14184.18s)]
*  These acts violate the duty to protect access to education in conflict-affected areas. [[03:56:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14193.18s)]
*  Second, Article 59 requires the occupying power to facilitate the delivery of humanitarian relief, especially when local resources are insufficient. [[03:56:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14200.18s)]
*  The occupying power has imposed a total siege on Gaza and has systematically obstructed humanitarian aid, especially that delivered by UNRWA. [[03:56:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14212.18s)]
*  Access points at Rafah, Karam Abu Salim, and north of Gaza were closed. [[03:57:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14223.18s)]
*  Though briefly eased during the latest ceasefire agreement, restrictions were fully reinstated in March 2025, halting all supplies, including water access. [[03:57:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14230.18s)]
*  The obstruction of aid operation not only breaches international obligations, but may also constitute collective punishment, which is strictly prohibited under Article 33 of the Fourth Geneva Convention. [[03:57:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14243.18s)]
*  Furthermore, Article 63 demands that the occupying power respects the work of humanitarian organizations, something the occupying power has consistently failed to do. [[03:57:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14257.18s)]
*  Third, the prohibition against the use of starvation as a method of warfare is firmly entrenched as a rule of customary international law and constitutes a war crime. [[03:57:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14271.18s)]
*  It is unequivocally prohibited under the statutes and jurisprudence of international criminal courts and tribunals. [[03:58:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14284.18s)]
*  Pursuant to Articles 55 and 59 of the Fourth Geneva Convention, the occupying power is legally obliged to guarantee the civilian population's access to food, water, and essential provisions, [[03:58:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14292.18s)]
*  and to facilitate humanitarian assistance if local resources are insufficient. [[03:58:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14310.18s)]
*  Any deliberate interference with aid deliveries, including food, medical supplies, and clean water, is thus a violation of this obligation, severely endangering civilian lives. [[03:58:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14316.18s)]
*  It is deeply concerning that since March 2025, the occupying power has again resorted explicitly to starvation as a deliberate policy measure. [[03:58:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14331.18s)]
*  In this context, it is noteworthy that the occupying power's reenactment of recent measures constitutes another strong indication that the occupying power latently disregards the court's provisional measure order dated 28 March 2024 and the genocide case wrote by South Africa against the occupying power. [[03:59:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14343.18s)]
*  Fourth, the occupying power must protect humanitarian personnel and facilities. [[03:59:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14369.18s)]
*  Article 71-2 of the Protocol Additional to the Geneva Conventions of 12 August 1949 and relating to the protection of victims of international armed conflicts prohibits attacks, harassment, or arbitrary detention of relief workers. [[03:59:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14375.18s)]
*  The occupying power's targeting of UNRWA premises, aid convoys, and medical staff constitutes a serious breach of this obligation and may amount to a war crime under customary international law. [[03:59:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14394.18s)]
*  Fifth, under Articles 18, 20, and 56 of the Fourth Geneva Convention, hospitals, medical staff, and healthcare infrastructure are to be protected at all times. [[04:00:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14411.18s)]
*  Deliberate attacks on these institutions and restrictions on evacuations and medical aid have severely undermined the already fragile healthcare system in Gaza. [[04:00:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14425.18s)]
*  In this context, the occupying power has impeded the entry of healthcare personnel, essential medicines, and critical medical supplies into Gaza. [[04:00:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14438.18s)]
*  Concurrently, it has been prevented and delayed the safe evacuation of patients by international organizations and third states. [[04:00:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14448.18s)]
*  Mr. President, the Court has also confirmed that international human rights law continues to apply during situations of occupation, including in the OPT. [[04:00:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14459.18s)]
*  The occupying power remains bound by its obligations under the International Covenant on Civil and Political Rights and the International Covenant on Economic, Social, and Cultural Rights to which it is a party. [[04:01:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14472.18s)]
*  The right to life enshrined in Article 6 of the ICCPR is absolute and non-derogable. [[04:01:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14487.18s)]
*  Restrictions on lifesaving aid and attacks targeting civilians constitute clear violations of this fundamental right. [[04:01:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14495.18s)]
*  The rights to food and water, core components of the right to an adequate standard of living as recognized in Articles 11 and 12 of the ICE-SCR, have been systematically undermined by the occupying power's destruction of critical infrastructure and obstruction of humanitarian access. [[04:01:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14505.18s)]
*  Similarly, the right to the highest attainable standard of physical and mental health, also guaranteed by the same Covenant, has been violated through repeated attacks on hospitals, the denial of medical evacuations, and the deliberate restriction of lifesaving medical supplies. [[04:02:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14527.18s)]
*  Equally, the right to education set forth in Article 13 of the same human rights instrument and reaffirmed in Article 50 of the Fourth Geneva Convention has likewise been gravely impaired by the widespread destruction of schools, forced displacement, and targeted assaults on educational institutions. [[04:02:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14547.18s)]
*  As far as children are concerned, pursuant to Article 6-2 of the Convention on the Rights of the Child, states parties are required to take all feasible measures to ensure the survival and development of children to the greatest extent possible. [[04:02:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14572.18s)]
*  Accordingly, the occupying power bears a clear responsibility to ensure sufficient nutrition and protect the lives of children under its effective control. Deliberately causing malnutrition to hundreds of thousands of children is entirely unjustifiable and unequivocally prohibited under all circumstances. [[04:03:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14591.18s)]
*  Finally, the right to self-determination, a permanent norm of international law, underpins many of these obligations. The occupying power's sustained interference with Palestinian civil, political, and economic development, particularly through its assault on humanitarian infrastructure, represents a profound violation of this right. [[04:03:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14615.18s)]
*  The present advisory proceedings concern the obligations of the occupying power in relation to the presence and activities of the UN, other international organizations, and third states in relation to the OPT. [[04:04:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14640.18s)]
*  By clarifying these obligations and the legal consequences arising from their violation, the Court will offer indispensable guidance to the international community. [[04:04:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14655.18s)]
*  Kuwait expresses its full confidence that the Court's opinion will reinforce the rule of law, protect the integrity of the UN system, and reaffirm the inalienable rights of the Palestinian people. [[04:04:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14666.18s)]
*  Mr. President, Members of the Court, this concludes Kuwait's oral statement. [[04:04:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14676.18s)]
*  On behalf of the delegation of Kuwait, I wish to extend our sincere appreciation to the Court for their understanding of the rights of the Palestinian people. [[04:04:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14681.18s)]
*  I also extend my appreciation to the Court for its careful attention and to express our gratitude to the Registry and the interpreters for their invaluable support throughout these proceedings. [[04:04:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14691.18s)]
*  It has been an honor to be here today. [[04:05:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14701.18s)]
*  I thank the representative of Kuwait for his presentation. [[04:05:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14704.18s)]
*  I also thank the delegation of Kuwait for their understanding of the rights of the Palestinian people. [[04:05:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14709.18s)]
*  I also thank the delegation of Kuwait for their understanding of the rights of the Palestinian people. [[04:05:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14714.18s)]
*  I also thank the delegation of Kuwait for their understanding of the rights of the Palestinian people. [[04:05:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14719.18s)]
*  I also thank the delegation of Kuwait for their understanding of the rights of the Palestinian people. [[04:05:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14726.18s)]
*  I now present the delegation of Luxembourg to speak and call Mr. Tobias Schell. [[04:05:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14734.18s)]
*  Mr. President, Ladies and Gentlemen, Members of the Court, [[04:05:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14752.18s)]
*  It is an honor for me to present before you today, as an agent of the Government of Luxembourg, our oral observations in the context of the present request for consultative opinion. [[04:05:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14756.18s)]
*  By its participation, Luxembourg expresses its deep attachment to the international justice system and to the essential role that your Court plays in the affirmation and application of the rules that govern this system. [[04:06:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14767.18s)]
*  The participation of Luxembourg in the context of the present request reflects its willingness to contribute to the strengthening of the international order founded on the rule of law, for which your Court dreamed of an essential role. [[04:06:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14782.18s)]
*  The solicited consultative opinion is included in the continuity of the one made by your Court on July 19, 2024, concerning the legal consequences of Israel's policies and practices in the occupied Palestinian territories, including East Jerusalem. [[04:06:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14800.18s)]
*  In this opinion, your Court has observed the elicited presence of Israel in the occupied Palestinian territories and has affirmed the obligation for Israel to put an end to this elicited presence in the shortest possible time. [[04:07:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14820.18s)]
*  In particular, in regards to the prolonged occupation of the TPO, which has persisted since 1967, your Court has observed that the Israeli state, acting as an occupying power, holds a set of powers and responsibilities towards the territory on which it exerts an effective control. [[04:07:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14838.18s)]
*  The solicited consultative opinion would allow you to complete and deepen the legal conclusions to which your Court has come in the 2024 consultative opinion and to clarify the specific obligations of Israel in terms of the presence and activities of the United Nations in the TPO in connection with it. [[04:07:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14864.18s)]
*  The legal conclusions of this opinion will serve as a foundation for analyzing the obligations of Israel in the context of the present consultative procedure. [[04:08:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14890.18s)]
*  Since the terrible terrorist attacks perpetrated by Hamas on October 7, 2023, and the capture of more than 200 hostages by Hamas, the humanitarian situation in the Gaza Strip, but also in the rest of the TPO, has dramatically worsened. [[04:08:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14902.18s)]
*  The rapid deterioration of the living conditions of the Palestinian population requires that your Court examine, as a priority and of utmost urgency, the additional questions raised by the General Assembly in order to clarify the obligations of Israel as a member state of the UN and occupying power in terms of the presence and activities of the UN in the TPO. [[04:08:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14921.18s)]
*  It is understood that the current oral observations limit themselves to answering the legal questions posed to the Court in terms of Israel's legal obligations, without prejudging the possible responsibilities of other actors. [[04:09:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14951.18s)]
*  In terms of the reliability of the request, Luxembourg believes that your Court is competent to respond to the request for a consultation from the General Assembly, and that it should be entitled to it, given the absence of decisive reasons to oppose a refusal. [[04:09:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14973.18s)]
*  In terms of the bottom line, Luxembourg wishes to present some observations on the legal points raised in the questions posed to your Court. [[04:09:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=14994.18s)]
*  The obligations of Israel must be examined at two distinct levels, as occupying power exercising effective control over the TPO and as a member state of the United Nations. [[04:10:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15004.18s)]
*  The obligations of Israel concern the presence and activities of the UN in the TPO of unlimited flows, international and charter organizations, humanitarian international law, international human rights and international customary law. [[04:10:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15016.18s)]
*  It is now clearly established that Israel remains the occupying power in the TPO, including the West Bank of Jordan, including East Jerusalem and the Gaza Strip. [[04:10:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15035.18s)]
*  The occupation is, in essence, a temporary situation. It would not be justified in transfer of sovereignty. [[04:10:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15048.18s)]
*  The quality of occupying power imposes to Israel a set of legal obligations that subsist, regardless of any consideration related to the length and duration of the occupation. [[04:10:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15057.18s)]
*  In this regard, your Court has highlighted that the obligations that occur in the international and international events that elicit from Israel do not dispense them from their continued duty to abandon the international obligations to which their behavior is subject. [[04:11:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15072.18s)]
*  In particular, Israel remains committed to observing the obligation that it embodies to respect the right of the Palestinian people to self-determination and the obligations to which it is committed in the regard of international humanitarian law and international law related to human rights. [[04:11:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15090.18s)]
*  The powers and duties of Israel, in the exercise of its responsibilities as occupying power in the TPO, are governed by international humanitarian law, and in particular the regulation of the AED of 1907, which is part of international customary law, imposes itself on Israel, although it is not part of contracting the fourth Geneva Convention of 1949, as well as international customary law. [[04:11:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15107.18s)]
*  Israel has, as occupying power, the general obligation to manage the territory occupied in the interest of the local population. This obligation comes from Article 43 of the AED. [[04:12:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15137.18s)]
*  This obligation also relies on the right to self-determination. [[04:12:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15151.18s)]
*  In the consultative report of 2024, your course stated that the dependence of the West Jordanian Sea, and more particularly the Gaza Strip, on Israel for the supply of essential goods and services, has an obstacle to the jouissance of fundamental human rights, in particular the right to self-determination. [[04:12:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15156.18s)]
*  However, Israel is united, by virtue of the right to self-determination, of which the Palestinian people enjoy, to take measures aimed at reducing this dependence, in particular by authorizing and facilitating the supply of essential goods and services by the United Nations. [[04:13:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15181.18s)]
*  By virtue of Article 55 of the fourth Geneva Convention, Israel is united to ensure the supply of the population of the TPO with the first essential necessities at the time of survival when the local resources are insufficient. [[04:13:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15199.18s)]
*  As you have observed in your consultative report of 2024, the occupying power has the continued obligation to ensure that the local population has adequate access to food, including water supply. [[04:13:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15217.18s)]
*  The primary responsibility of the supply of humanitarian aid therefore falls on the part of the power of which the civilians and other protected persons are. [[04:13:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15234.18s)]
*  However, if their essential needs cannot be met in this way, the party in power, its adversary, and the state-owned enterprises must allow external actors to provide humanitarian aid under certain conditions. [[04:14:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15245.18s)]
*  Article 59 of the fourth Geneva Convention includes two obligations. [[04:14:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15263.18s)]
*  On the one hand, the obligation to accept aid actions, and on the other hand, the obligation to facilitate these actions in all the measure of these means. [[04:14:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15269.18s)]
*  These obligations have an unconditional nature. [[04:14:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15280.18s)]
*  The occupying power would not be able to withstand it as long as it is established that the population of the occupied territory is insufficiently provided. [[04:14:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15284.18s)]
*  These collective aid actions could be undertaken by states or impartial humanitarian organizations. [[04:14:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15294.18s)]
*  Although the occupying power has a certain level of appreciation for the acceptance and facilitation of humanitarian aid, it remains committed to taking into account the real needs of the population of the occupied territory, as well as the available resources to provide humanitarian assistance. [[04:15:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15303.18s)]
*  Luxembourg has to emphasize the indispensable role played by the United Nations agencies and programs in providing essential humanitarian assistance to the civilian population of the TPO, and in particular the vital role of the UNRWA. [[04:15:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15326.18s)]
*  Its essential role in providing humanitarian assistance to Palestinian refugees through the essential education, health, aid, social services and emergency aid programs has been recognized by the Security Council, which has described it as the backbone of all humanitarian interventions in Gaza. [[04:15:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15343.18s)]
*  It has also emphasized that no organization can replace or replace the capacity and mandate of UNRWA to serve Palestinian refugees and civilians who need urgent humanitarian assistance. [[04:16:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15366.18s)]
*  The unchangeable and vital role of UNRWA has also been highlighted by the General Assembly in its resolution of the UNRWA 1025. [[04:16:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15382.18s)]
*  UNRWA is the main supplier of humanitarian aid and essential services in the TPO. [[04:16:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15393.18s)]
*  In regard to the extreme gravity of the humanitarian crisis in the Gaza Strip and to the lack of alternatives that have the capacity required to provide adequate provision for the population, [[04:16:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15400.18s)]
*  it is an important task for Israel, in its capacity as an occupying power, to facilitate access without hindrance to the UNRWA agencies, including UNRWA, to humanitarian aid, in accordance with Article 59 of the Fourth Convention of Geneva. [[04:16:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15413.18s)]
*  Article 59, paragraph 3, imposes to all states contracting Israel's part, the obligation to authorize the free passage of the couriers and, in a complementary manner, the obligation to ensure protection. [[04:17:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15431.18s)]
*  Article 59, paragraph 9, paragraph 4, contains a safeguard clause allowing the occupying power to exercise its right to inspect and control the sending of its couriers and to monitor the distribution. [[04:17:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15449.18s)]
*  The technical provisions prescribed must however not be subject to the obligation to ensure the rapid passage and without hindrance of its couriers, as your course on the situation in Gaza affirmed. [[04:17:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15466.18s)]
*  Israel would not, however, exercise its right to inspect and control in an abusive or arbitrary manner to make the principle itself unapparent, or to delay the release of its couriers. [[04:18:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15480.18s)]
*  As the UN Secretary General has highlighted in his press release on April 8, 2025, the mechanisms of authorization recently proposed by the Israeli authorities for the release of risk aid, to limit aid without hindrance, while at the point of passage, food, medicine and shelter are accumulated and vital equipment are blocked. [[04:18:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15496.18s)]
*  The obligation to allow the free passage of humanitarian aid is complemented by the obligation to protect aid and humanitarian personnel, a rule that is dedicated to international and customary law. [[04:18:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15523.18s)]
*  In order for humanitarian aid to be provided to the civilian population, the security of humanitarian personnel who provide this aid must be ensured. [[04:18:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15538.18s)]
*  The personnel of this course are protected against attacks by the principle of distinction. [[04:19:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15548.18s)]
*  The practice not only emphasizes the prohibition of attacks against humanitarian personnel, but also that of harassment, intimidation and arbitrary detention at their encounter. [[04:19:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15554.18s)]
*  And announces, as an example, the condemned acts committed against humanitarian personnel. [[04:19:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15569.18s)]
*  Bad treatment, physical and moral violence, murder, coup, kidnapping, hostage-taking, harassment, theft, arrest and illegal detention. [[04:19:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15576.18s)]
*  The Security Council regularly recalls the need for parties in conflict to respect and protect humanitarian personnel. [[04:19:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15587.18s)]
*  In its Resolution 2730 of May 24, 2024, the Security Council has condemned without any doubt the fact of targeting the members of humanitarian personnel in the exercise of their functions, [[04:19:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15598.18s)]
*  to kill them, to harass them, to subject them to pursuits, to arbitrary arrests or arbitrary detentions. [[04:20:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15613.18s)]
*  According to the figures communicated by the United Nations Humanitarian Affairs Coordination Office on February 18, 2025, [[04:20:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15621.18s)]
*  at least 384 humanitarian workers have been killed in the Gaza Strip since the beginning of the war in October 2003, [[04:20:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15629.18s)]
*  of which 277 were employees of the United Nations, most of whom were part of the UNRWA personnel. [[04:20:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15639.18s)]
*  As for humanitarian personnel, the goods used for humanitarian aid must also be respected and protected by international customary law, [[04:20:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15648.18s)]
*  yet it is entitled to the protection that international humanitarian law guarantees to civil-character goods. [[04:21:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15660.18s)]
*  Article 56, paragraph 1 of the 4th Convention of Geneva, [[04:21:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15670.18s)]
*  predicts that, in all the measure of these means, the occupying power will have the duty to ensure and maintain, [[04:21:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15674.18s)]
*  with the help of national and local authorities, the establishments and medical and hospital services, [[04:21:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15681.18s)]
*  as well as public health and hygiene in the occupied territory, [[04:21:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15688.18s)]
*  and that the medical personnel of all categories will be authorized to accomplish their mission. [[04:21:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15693.18s)]
*  It is not doubted that the hospitals and health centers of the UNRWA, and more generally health activities run by the UNRWA, [[04:21:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15702.18s)]
*  can be classified as establishments and medical services. [[04:21:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15710.18s)]
*  The occupying power has the obligation to ensure and maintain these establishments and medical services, [[04:21:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15714.18s)]
*  which forces them to take all necessary measures to ensure that these establishments carry out their work well. [[04:22:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15721.18s)]
*  As for the occupying power, it involves the obligation for Israel to abstain from taking measures that would force the health and health centers of the UNRWA [[04:22:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15729.18s)]
*  to end their activities or to end their infrastructure. [[04:22:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15740.18s)]
*  This also involves facilitating the movement of medical personnel without hindrance, [[04:22:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15746.18s)]
*  facilitating the delivery of medical supplies and equipment in the TPO, [[04:22:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15752.18s)]
*  and the possibility for the health and health personnel of the UNRWA to provide medical care to the injured and the sick. [[04:22:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15758.18s)]
*  Article 50, paragraph 1 of the 4th Geneva Convention, [[04:22:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15766.18s)]
*  provides that the occupying power will facilitate, with the competition of national and local authorities, [[04:22:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15770.18s)]
*  the proper functioning of the establishments dedicated to the care and education of children. [[04:22:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15776.18s)]
*  The activities of these institutions must therefore not be hindered by the occupying power. [[04:23:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15783.18s)]
*  As for the TPO, it involves the obligation for Israel to abstain from detaining the staff of the UNRWA schools, [[04:23:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15791.18s)]
*  to use these schools for military operations or to endow their locals. [[04:23:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15800.18s)]
*  The occupying power is not only to abstain from any action that would prevent the activities of these institutions, [[04:23:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15807.18s)]
*  but also to actively support them if the national authorities responsible are failing. [[04:23:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15814.18s)]
*  It must, in particular, facilitate the repair of damaged schools, facilitate the production of the necessary supplies [[04:23:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15821.18s)]
*  for educational activities or even secure the initiatives to allow children to access schools. [[04:23:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15829.18s)]
*  The obligation to facilitate the proper functioning of the institutions dedicated to the care and education of children, [[04:23:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15837.18s)]
*  as provided in article 50, paragraph 1, [[04:24:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15843.18s)]
*  must be interpreted jointly with other rules of humanitarian international law, [[04:24:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15846.18s)]
*  which include the well-being of children, [[04:24:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15851.18s)]
*  such as article 24 of the 4th Geneva Convention, [[04:24:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15854.18s)]
*  and the obligation, by virtue of the international customary law, [[04:24:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15857.18s)]
*  to give respect and protection to children affected by an armed conflict. [[04:24:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15860.18s)]
*  The obligations of states in the field of human rights also apply when the state exerts its sovereignty outside its territory, [[04:24:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15867.18s)]
*  in particular in occupying situations. [[04:24:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15876.18s)]
*  Your course has reminded us that the main international instruments relating to human rights, [[04:24:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15880.18s)]
*  the International Pact on Civil and Political Rights, [[04:24:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15886.18s)]
*  the International Pact on Economic, Social and Cultural Rights, [[04:24:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15889.18s)]
*  the International Convention on the Elimination of All Forms of Racial Discrimination, [[04:24:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15893.18s)]
*  and the Convention on the Rights of the Child, [[04:24:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15899.18s)]
*  to which Israel and other parties are applicable in the TPO. [[04:25:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15902.18s)]
*  As your course has highlighted several times, [[04:25:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15908.18s)]
*  the protection offered by the conventions governing human rights does not cease in case of armed conflict or occupation. [[04:25:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15912.18s)]
*  The international humanitarian law and the international human rights law are complementary and must be taken into account simultaneously. [[04:25:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15920.18s)]
*  The instruments mentioned are enclosed in a set of dispositions applicable in the context of the supply of humanitarian aid in the TPO, [[04:25:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15929.18s)]
*  and concern in particular the right to life, the right of every person to be sheltered from hunger, [[04:25:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15938.18s)]
*  the right to a sufficient level of life for each person and their family, [[04:25:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15944.18s)]
*  including all food, clothing and sufficient accommodation, the right to health and the right to water. [[04:25:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15948.18s)]
*  It should be noted that the international pact on social and cultural economic rights [[04:25:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15957.18s)]
*  is the law of the UN. Israel enjoys a number of rights but also assumes duties. [[04:26:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15992.18s)]
*  The resolution 273 of May 11, 1949, by which the UN General Assembly admitted Israel as a member of the UN, [[04:26:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=15997.18s)]
*  specifies that it accepts without reservation any. [[04:26:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16007.18s)]
*  The obligations that come from the Charter and commit to respect them from the day it becomes a member of the UN. [[04:26:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16012.18s)]
*  According to my disposition of the Charter, Israel, as any member of the UN, [[04:27:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16021.18s)]
*  is held to an obligation of assistance in the UN that it must be fulfilled with good faith. [[04:27:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16026.18s)]
*  This is also true for the UN agencies that are an integral part of the UN system. [[04:27:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16033.18s)]
*  Given the factual circumstances that led to the seizure of the Charter, [[04:27:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16041.18s)]
*  namely the adoption by the Knesset on October 28, 2024, of two laws aimed at banning the activities of UNRWA, [[04:27:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16045.18s)]
*  the following analysis will essentially carry out on the presence and activities of these agencies in the TPO. [[04:27:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16054.18s)]
*  The privileges and immunity necessary to the action of the UN and its agencies on the territory of each of these Member States [[04:27:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16060.18s)]
*  are protected in accordance with Article 105 of the Charter. [[04:27:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16069.18s)]
*  The privileges and immunity that the UNRWA enjoys are defined in more detail in the general convention [[04:27:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16074.18s)]
*  on the privileges and immunity of the United Nations in 1946, to which Israel was assigned in 1949. [[04:28:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16080.18s)]
*  As a member of the UNRWA, Israel is held to respect the obligations in the matter of the privileges and immunity that come with it. [[04:28:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16088.18s)]
*  According to Section 35 of the General Convention, Member States cannot denounce this Convention as long as they are members of the UNRWA. [[04:28:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16099.18s)]
*  As for UNRWA specifically, the General Assembly reiterated repeatedly the application of the General Convention to this agency [[04:28:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16110.18s)]
*  and reminded that Israel is held to respect the UNRWA mandate as well as its privileges and immunity. [[04:28:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16122.18s)]
*  As a subsidiary body of the UNRWA, UNRWA benefits from the same immunities and privileges in all its Member States, including Israel. [[04:28:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16130.18s)]
*  In the exchange of letters, as Michel More concluded in 1967, [[04:29:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16141.18s)]
*  Israel acknowledged that the General Convention was in charge of the relations between the Israeli government and UNRWA regarding the exercise of functions of the agency. [[04:29:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16146.18s)]
*  The laws of October 28-24 foretell the abrogation of the so-called agreement and the revocation of the privileges and immunity granted to UNRWA. [[04:29:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16155.18s)]
*  However, it should be noted that this exchange of letters could not constitute the legal basis of the presence of UNRWA or the UN on the Israeli territory. [[04:29:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16164.18s)]
*  This is the pre-existing conclusion of the provisional agreement. [[04:29:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16174.18s)]
*  The agreement does not create the immunity privileges of UNRWA, but only recognizes their existence. [[04:29:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16178.18s)]
*  As a result, the resiliation of the agreement would not deprive the Agency of immunity privileges which it enjoys through the General Convention. [[04:29:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16185.18s)]
*  According to Section 34 of the General Convention, Israel must be able to apply the provisions of the Convention by virtue of its own rights. [[04:29:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16194.18s)]
*  It cannot invoke the provisions of its internal law as justifying the non-execution of obligations. [[04:30:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16205.18s)]
*  It is clear that the internal laws of Israel, including the laws of the Knesset, must be implemented in a way that is compatible with the international obligations of Israel by virtue of the Convention. [[04:30:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16212.18s)]
*  Luxembourg considers that certain provisions of the laws adopted by the Knesset are likely, if they are implemented, to violate the obligations of Israel under Article 105 of the Charter and the General Convention. [[04:30:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16226.18s)]
*  By virtue of these laws, any contact between the employees of Israel and UNRWA or through an intermediary is prohibited. [[04:30:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16242.18s)]
*  This makes it impossible for the Agency to exercise its functions without contacting the Israeli authorities, especially regarding the delivery of visas to its staff. [[04:30:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16251.18s)]
*  This measure goes against the obligation of assistance that Israel owes to the UN and its organizations by virtue of the Charter. [[04:31:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16268.18s)]
*  The laws of the Knesset also suggest that criminal pursuits against UNRWA staff cannot be excluded. [[04:31:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16277.18s)]
*  If the scope of this arrangement does not seem to be clear, it is important to note that any criminal pursuit committed by Israel against UNRWA staff would be incompatible with the Convention that grants an immunity of jurisdiction to UN officials for the acts carried out by them in the exercise of their functions. [[04:31:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16286.18s)]
*  According to Section 20 of the Convention, the immunity of UN officials could be raised to the decision of the UN. [[04:31:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16310.18s)]
*  If Israel wishes to raise this immunity in particular cases, it should demand it from the UN and motivate it. [[04:31:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16319.18s)]
*  In invoking the laws of the Knesset, Israel demanded that UNRWA stop its activities in Jerusalem and leave all its staff until the 30th of January 2025, although this is incompatible with the inviolability of UNRWA staff. [[04:32:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16331.18s)]
*  It is good to have these assets under the section 3 of the Convention. [[04:32:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16351.18s)]
*  The inviolability of UNRWA staff is absolute. [[04:32:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16356.18s)]
*  It cannot be excluded for the reasons that, in particular circumstances of hostilities, the inviolability of UNRWA staff and goods should be restricted or replaced by military opportunities. [[04:32:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16360.18s)]
*  The Charter and the Convention do not admit any reserve in this regard. [[04:32:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16378.18s)]
*  It is the result of what precedes that Israel's demands regarding UNRWA's stop its activities, the evacuation of its staff and the loss of immunity and inviolability in Jewish staff and staff, if they are implemented, go against Israel's legal obligations to the Charter and the Convention. [[04:33:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16382.18s)]
*  The UN and its staff, including UNRWA, must continue to benefit from the privileges and immunities necessary to accomplish their mission. [[04:33:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16407.18s)]
*  Luxembourg considers, therefore, that the laws of the Knesset are incompatible with the obligations of Israel, in virtue of international law. [[04:33:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16418.18s)]
*  Their implementation would, as a consequence, prevent UNRWA from continuing its essential activities in the Charter, thus putting the unique and irreplaceable mandate conferred on the agency in danger. [[04:33:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16427.18s)]
*  Mr. President, Ladies and Gentlemen, Members of the Court, allow me to make a few final remarks. [[04:34:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16444.18s)]
*  The legal obligations that [[04:34:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16451.18s)]
*  are in the hands of Israel, both as occupying power in the Charter and as a member of the United Nations, [[04:34:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16453.98s)]
*  require cooperation with the United Nations agencies, including UNRWA, to ensure the continuity of humanitarian operations in the Charter. [[04:34:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16460.18s)]
*  The respect of these obligations is even more imperative in the face of the dramatic humanitarian urgency that is taking place in the Gaza Strip. [[04:34:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16470.18s)]
*  The survival of hundreds of thousands of civilians depends on access to humanitarian aid. [[04:34:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16479.18s)]
*  The access of the United Nations in the Charter, particularly through UNRWA, is essential and indispensable, [[04:34:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16485.18s)]
*  both in terms of the progression of humanitarian aid and the basic service provision, such as health and education. [[04:34:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16492.18s)]
*  At this end, the role of UNRWA, recognized by the international community as irreplaceable, must be fully protected. [[04:35:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16502.18s)]
*  As occupying power, Israel is held by international humanitarian law to administer the TPO in the interest of the local population, [[04:35:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16510.18s)]
*  particularly by providing humanitarian aid to the civilian population and by facilitating the actions of these courses organized by the TPO in the United Nations agencies. [[04:35:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16520.18s)]
*  This also involves allowing the free passage of humanitarian aid and ensuring their protection. [[04:35:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16532.18s)]
*  As a member of the UNRWA, Israel must facilitate and protect the presence of UNRWA activities and these organs, [[04:35:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16539.18s)]
*  particularly by respecting the applicable immunities. [[04:35:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16546.18s)]
*  Mr. President, Madam Members of the Court, this concludes my intervention and I thank you for your attention. [[04:35:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16551.18s)]
*  I thank the representative of the UNRWA for her presentation, which will be held in the audience this afternoon. [[04:36:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vbR9CQVAMV4&t=16562.18s)]
